create table `xy_migrations` (`id` int unsigned not null auto_increment primary key, `migration` varchar(255) not null, `batch` int not null) default character set utf8mb4 collate 'utf8mb4_unicode_ci'

select max(`batch`) as aggregate from `xy_migrations`

create table `xy_migrations` (`id` int unsigned not null auto_increment primary key, `migration` varchar(255) not null, `batch` int not null) default character set utf8mb4 collate 'utf8mb4_unicode_ci'

select max(`batch`) as aggregate from `xy_migrations`
